worker pane productive every cycle. You may NEVER respond to a blocker, a

is NORMAL and EXPECTED in this parallel factory — lanes have disjoint
write scope precisely so a globally-clean tree is never required. "Tree
dirty" / "boundary moved" / "waiting on a VALIDATOR/GM/REVIEWER lease" are
NOT stop conditions and NEVER justify holding a pane. If a worker's current
atom is genuinely blocked, RE-TASK that pane immediately to the next
independent unblocked Phase-A SOURCE-EXPANSION atom or a CONTENT-VERIFY
atom — do not sleep it. An idle/held pane is a P0 MANAGER defect to fix
this cycle, not an acceptable state. The only thing that may block a *push*
is a hard correctness failure (tsc error, test:content red, a content gate
red); that still never blocks a *pane* from moving to other work.
PHASE-B IS DEFERRED BY OPERATOR (2026-05-18): Phase-B (non-UHR / external

SOURCE-EXPANSION [content, P0 program, target = 2000 verified questions]:
  PHASE A — EXHAUST UHR: mine the UHR "Sverige i fokus" material
  completely. Every distinct fact/concept/topic in every UHR chapter &
  section must yield question(s) until UHR coverage is SATURATED (no
  remaining UHR fact a fair test could ask that we don't cover). Add a
  UHR-coverage report/check: per UHR chapter+section, list facts vs
  questions; gaps are tracked and burned down.
  PHASE B — EXPAND SAME TOPICS FROM OTHER AUTHORITIES: within the SAME
  UHR topic domains, add questions researched from OTHER authoritative
  public sources, e.g. riksdagen.se / lagen.nu (law), regeringen.se,
  Skatteverket, Migrationsverket, SCB, Skolverket, Forsakringskassan,
  1177, Arbetsformedlingen, Pensionsmyndigheten, MSB/krisinformation.se,
  Sweden.se / Swedish Institute, official kommun/region .se pages. Prefer
  primary official sources over secondary.
  TARGET: ramp the bank to ~2000 questions total, balanced across all
  civic domains and difficulty (Latt/Medel/Svar), NO near-duplicate
  stems/answers (reuse the duplicate-text detector; dup = reject).
  STRICT CITATION GATE (executable, hard, per question — uncited or
  unverifiable = P0, NOT shippable): every question MUST carry a
  specific verifiable public source — concrete source title + locator
  (chapter/section/page or stable public URL), not a vague 'official
  info'. That citation MUST render to the user on the website (the
  Kalla/Source line under the question). Add/extend a test asserting:
  (a) 100% of questions have a non-empty, well-formed verifiable source;
  (b) the source string is surfaced in the rendered question UI. A
  question whose fact cannot be traced to a citable public source is
  deleted, not guessed. Factually wrong/outdated = P0.
  PROVENANCE LABEL (executable, hard): every question has a required
  provenance field marking its origin as either the official UHR study
  material ("Sverige i fokus") or an EXTERNAL authority. Every non-UHR
  question MUST show a clear, localized label/badge in the rendered UI
  (SV+EN, e.g. "Extern kalla - utover UHR-materialet" / "External
  source - beyond the UHR material") so the learner always knows which
  questions come from the official study material vs supplementary
  authoritative sources. UHR-origin questions are NOT given the external
  label. This label is IN ADDITION to (never a replacement for) the
  specific Kalla/Source citation line. Add/extend a test asserting:
  (a) 100% of questions have a valid provenance value (uhr|external);
  (b) every external-provenance question renders the external label in
  the question UI; (c) no UHR question is mislabeled external. A non-UHR
  question without the visible external label = P0, not shippable.
  QUALITY (unchanged, all still enforced): original PARAPHRASED wording
  (never verbatim source text), natural fluent language, SV+EN parity
  now (then the EBOOK multilingual set), not-a-real-exam disclaimer, no
  claimed official affiliation, DESIGN.md tokens, all content gates green.
  PROCESS: incremental atoms (~25-50 fully-sourced verified questions per
  atom), id-sequence continues, regenerate question-bank.csv, run
  test:content each atom (never push red). Grow coverage; never dilute
  accuracy or citation rigour to hit the count.

SHUFFLE-FIX [DONE 2026-05-18 — verified on origin/main]: implemented in lib/quiz/answerOptionShuffle.ts (seeded Fisher-Yates keyed by question+session, stable within a session) + summarize/balance checks, wired into lib/quiz/examGenerator.ts, practiceSessionStore.ts, app/quiz/[sessionId].tsx, app/(tabs)/practice.tsx. SHUFFLE-FIX-HIST [P0, correctness]: Single-choice answer options are NOT shuffled —
data/questions.ts authored with correct answer mostly first (correctOptionId
'a' dominant) and lib/content/derivedQuestions.ts normalizeSingleChoiceOptions
maps by index with no randomization, so the correct answer is almost always A.
This makes the quiz trivially gameable and looks broken.
FIX (root cause, in the derivation/session pipeline, NOT a data-only patch):
- Shuffle single-choice options with a SEEDED RNG keyed by (questionId +
  sessionId) so order is randomized but STABLE within a quiz session/instance
  (must NOT reshuffle on re-render or change mid-question), and reproducible
  for review screens and tests.
- Remap correctOptionId after shuffle; isCorrectAnswer must still resolve
  correctly; explanations/option feedback follow the option, not the slot.
- Exclude true_false from positional shuffle (keep true/false order fixed).
- Interacts with DIFFICULTY-1: pick distractors by difficulty FIRST, then
  shuffle the final option set.
TESTS (add, must pass): over the full published bank, correct-answer display
  position is ~uniform (no single position > 35%); shuffle stable within a
  session; isCorrectAnswer correct post-shuffle. Keep all 7 acceptance steps
  green. This is the highest-priority item in this file.

questionEn pairs in types/content.ts with
questionText: Record<LocaleCode, string> (same for options and explanations).

PracticeQuestion. uhrReference becomes optional when provenance !== 'uhr'.
